<p><b>Paul Labile Pogba</b> (born 15 March 1993) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a>. He operates primarily as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, but can also be deployed as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a> and <a href="/wiki/Playmaker#Deep-lying_playmakers" title="Playmaker">deep-lying playmaker</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Paul_Pogba_(Manchester_United_FC)_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paul_Pogba_(Manchester_United_FC)-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Lagny-sur-Marne" title="Lagny-sur-Marne">Lagny-sur-Marne</a>, Pogba joined the youth team of <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> side <a href="/wiki/Le_Havre_AC" title="Le Havre AC">Le Havre</a> in 2007, before a protracted transfer brought him to Manchester United two years later. After beginning his senior career with Manchester United two years later, limited appearances persuaded him to depart to join Italian side <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> on a free transfer in 2012, where he helped the club to four consecutive <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> titles, as well as two <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> and two <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> titles. During his time in Italy, Pogba further established himself as one of the most promising young players in the world and received the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Boy_(award)" title="Golden Boy (award)">Golden Boy</a> award in 2013, followed by the <a href="/wiki/Bravo_Award" title="Bravo Award">Bravo Award</a> in 2014. In 2016, Pogba was named to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year#Team_of_the_Year_2015" title="UEFA Team of the Year">2015 UEFA Team of the Year</a>, as well as the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_World_XI" title="FIFPro">2015 FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>, after helping Juventus to the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">2015 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, their first in 12 years.
</p><p>Pogba's performances at Juventus led to him returning to Manchester United in 2016 for a then-<a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">world record transfer fee</a> of €105&#160;million (£89.3&#160;million).<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The fee paid for him remains the highest paid by an English club.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> In his first season back, he won the <a href="/wiki/2017_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2017 EFL Cup Final">League Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Europa League Final">Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Premier_League" title="2018–19 Premier League">2018–19</a> season, he was named to the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a>.
</p><p>Internationally, he captained France to victory at the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a> and took home the award for the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup#Awards" title="2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup">Best Player</a> for his performances during the tournament. He made his debut for the <a href="/wiki/French_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="French national football team">senior team</a> a year later and featured prominently at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, where he was awarded the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Best_Young_Player" title="2014 FIFA World Cup awards">Best Young Player Award</a> for his performances. He later represented his nation at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> on home soil, where he finished as a runner-up, before winning the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, scoring the winning goal in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h2>
<p>Pogba was born in <a href="/wiki/Lagny-sur-Marne" title="Lagny-sur-Marne">Lagny-sur-Marne</a>, Seine-et-Marne, to Guinean parents.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He is Muslim.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He has two older brothers who are <a href="/wiki/Twins" class="mw-redirect" title="Twins">twins</a> – <a href="/wiki/Florentin_Pogba" title="Florentin Pogba">Florentin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mathias_Pogba" title="Mathias Pogba">Mathias</a> – born in Guinea, who are also footballers and play for the <a href="/wiki/Guinea_national_football_team" title="Guinea national football team">Guinean national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Florentin currently plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)" title="Defender (association football)">defender</a> for <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">FC Sochaux-Montbéliard</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> while Mathias plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for <a href="/wiki/NK_Tabor_Se%C5%BEana" title="NK Tabor Sežana">Tabor Sežana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Growing up, Pogba was a fan of <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint noexcerpt Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:NOTRS"><span title="tabloid (December 2020)">better&#160;source&#160;needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"<a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> is my footballing role model and the player that made me fall in love with football. I was enthralled by him as I used to play up front when I was younger."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Pogba on his idol, former Brazilian forward Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Pogba began his football career at the age of six playing for US Roissy-en-Brie, a few miles south of his hometown. He spent seven seasons at the club before joining <a href="/wiki/US_Torcy" title="US Torcy">US Torcy</a>, where he served as captain of the club's under-13 team.<sup id="cite_ref-pogba_torcy_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pogba_torcy-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After one season with Torcy, Pogba joined professional club <a href="/wiki/Le_Havre_AC" title="Le Havre AC">Le Havre</a>. In his second season at the club, Pogba captained its under-16 team to the final phase of its domestic league, the <i>Championnat National des 16 ans</i>. Le Havre finished second to <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a> in the final group phase, finishing ahead of the likes of <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais_Reserves_and_Academy" title="Olympique Lyonnais Reserves and Academy">Lyon</a> and <a href="/wiki/AS_Nancy" title="AS Nancy">Nancy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Pogba also established himself as a youth international for his country.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_United">Manchester United</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/2009_English_football_tapping_up_controversy" title="2009 English football tapping up controversy">2009 English football tapping up controversy</a></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Transfer">Transfer</span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:30%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"The player [Pogba] and his parents refused to keep the arrangement because Manchester United offered very high sums of money to the parents of the [player] with the aim of obtaining the transfer of their son."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><small><a href="/wiki/Le_Havre_AC" title="Le Havre AC">Le Havre</a>'s response to Pogba's decision to join <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pogba_departure_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pogba_departure-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> </small></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 31 July 2009, Pogba announced that he was departing Le Havre to join the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" title="Manchester United F.C. Reserves and Academy">youth academy</a> of <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in England. The move surprised his parent club, as it allegedly had a "non-solicitation agreement" with Pogba, which was agreed to by not only the player but also his parents in 2006. The agreement, which was in place until the end of the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_in_French_football" title="2009–10 in French football">2009–10 season</a>, allowed Le Havre to sign Pogba to an <i>aspirant</i> (youth) contract once the player met specific age and scholarship requirements.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 1 August, Le Havre released an official statement on its website criticising Manchester United and the Pogba family.<sup id="cite_ref-pogba_departure_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pogba_departure-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Le Havre also announced its intent to ask <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> to probe the situation.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In response to Le Havre's accusations, Manchester United threatened to sue the club, while Pogba denied he was leaving Le Havre for monetary reasons, which Le Havre President Jean-Pierre Louvel had alleged to be £87,000 and a house.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Le Havre was also accused by Pogba's former club Torcy of using the same tactics it purported Manchester United to have used when the club acquired Pogba from its youth academy. On the same day of Pogba's announcement to depart for England, Torcy released a press release on its official website criticising Le Havre's accusations, stating, "We will not use the term 'steal,' but the recruiters of Le Havre acted the same way with the club in Torcy." The club cited Le Havre's acceptance of allowing Pogba to sign an amateur licence with the club without notifying Torcy as its primary reason why.<sup id="cite_ref-pogba_torcy_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pogba_torcy-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 7 October, Manchester United were cleared of wrongdoing by a judge appointed by FIFA, with the declaration that Pogba was not contractually linked to Le Havre.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Despite having the option to appeal, on 18 June 2010, Le Havre officials confirmed that the club had reached an agreement with Manchester United for the transfer of Pogba. The terms of the agreement were confidential.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Academy_and_call_up_to_first_team">Academy and call up to first team</span></h4>
<p>Pogba completed his transfer to Manchester United on 7 October 2009<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> and made his debut with the club's under-18 team on 10 October against <a href="/wiki/Crewe_Alexandra_F.C." title="Crewe Alexandra F.C.">Crewe Alexandra</a> in a 2–1 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Premier_Academy_League" title="2009–10 Premier Academy League">2009–10 under-18 campaign</a> with seven goals in 21 appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The team finished first in their group, but lost to <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Academy">Arsenal</a> 5–3 on <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout" title="Penalty shootout">penalties</a> in the play-off semi-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> In April 2010, Pogba was a part of the under-18 team that successfully defended their title at the Torneo Calcio Memorial Claudio Sassi-Sassuolo in <a href="/wiki/Bologna" title="Bologna">Bologna</a>, Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_in_English_football" title="2010–11 in English football">2010–11 season</a>, Pogba remained on the club's academy team in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_Academy_League" title="Premier Academy League">Premier Academy League</a> and played with the team during the first three months of the season. In November 2010, he was called up to the club's <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" title="Manchester United F.C. Reserves and Academy">reserve team</a> and made his debut on 2 November 2010 in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Bolton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Bolton Wanderers F.C.">Bolton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 10 January 2011, in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_FA_Youth_Cup" title="2010–11 FA Youth Cup">FA Youth Cup</a>, Pogba scored a long-range goal, described as a "piledriver," in the team's 3–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth_F.C." title="Portsmouth F.C.">Portsmouth</a>. The win allowed the team to progress to the fourth round of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> A month later, Pogba scored a similar goal in a 3–2 defeat to <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> in the Academy League.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 February 2011, Pogba was one of four academy players promoted to the first-team squad by manager <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Alex Ferguson</a> ahead of Manchester United's <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> fifth round match against <a href="/wiki/Crawley_Town_F.C." title="Crawley Town F.C.">Crawley Town</a>, for which he was assigned the number 42 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> He continued in the under-18s for the rest of the season, helping the team to a lengthy run in the FA Youth Cup; in the semi-final encounter against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Chelsea F.C. Reserves and Academy">Chelsea</a> in the competition, Pogba scored a goal in the first leg, a 3–2 defeat,<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> and provided the assist for the opening goal of the second leg, a 4–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In the final, Manchester United defeated <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_United_F.C." title="Sheffield United F.C.">Sheffield United</a> 6–3 on aggregate to win their tenth Youth Cup title; Pogba started and played the entire match in both legs.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season:_Limited_senior_team_appearances"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–12_season:_Limited_senior_team_appearances">2011–12 season:  Limited senior team appearances</span></h4>
<p>Ahead of the start of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Premier_League" title="2011–12 Premier League">2011–12 season</a>, Ferguson confirmed that Pogba would feature with the senior team during the season, stating, "I mean if we hold Pogba back, what's going to happen? He's going to leave. You know, in a couple of years' time when his contract is going to finish. So we have to give him the opportunity to see how he can do in the first-team and he's got great ability."<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Pogba was promoted to the club's reserve team permanently for the 2011–12 season and made his first appearance of the season on 15 August 2011 in the team's opening <a href="/wiki/Premier_Reserve_League" title="Premier Reserve League">Premier Reserve League</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Reserves" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Reserves">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> On 25 August, in the team's second league match against <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City reserves</a>, Pogba scored the second goal in a 6–0 rout.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 19 September, he was named to the first team to participate in their <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Football_League_Cup" title="2011–12 Football League Cup">Football League Cup</a> tie against <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds United</a> the following day, with Ferguson proclaiming, "I intend to play him [Pogba] against Leeds United."<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Pogba appeared as a half-time substitute to make his professional debut as Manchester United won the match 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Pogba made his second appearance against <a href="/wiki/Aldershot_Town_F.C." title="Aldershot Town F.C.">Aldershot Town</a> in the Fourth Round of the League Cup on 25 October 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pogba made his <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> debut against <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a> on 31 January 2012, replacing <a href="/wiki/Javier_Hern%C3%A1ndez" title="Javier Hernández">Javier Hernández</a> in the 72nd minute.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He made another substitute appearance against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> on 11 March.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he made his [European debut in the second leg of the team's <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2011–12 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> round of 16 tie against Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>; he appeared as a substitute in the 2–1 away defeat, coming on for <a href="/wiki/Michael_Carrick" title="Michael Carrick">Michael Carrick</a> in the 63rd minute as Manchester United lost the tie 5–3 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Juventus">Juventus</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012–13_season">2012–13 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_Juventus_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg/220px-Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="251" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg/330px-Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg/440px-Paul_Pogba_Juventus_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="453" data-file-height="517" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_Juventus_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba playing for <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in 2012</div></div></div>
<p>On 3 July 2012, Manchester United manager Alex Ferguson confirmed that Pogba had left the club after not signing a new contract.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Ferguson stated that Pogba had signed for Italian club <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> "a long time ago as far as we're aware." Ferguson also accused Pogba of disrespecting Manchester United, saying, "It is disappointing. I don't think he showed us any respect at all, to be honest. I'm quite happy that if they [footballers] carry on that way, they're probably better doing it away from us."<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 27 July, Juventus confirmed on their official website that Pogba had undergone a medical at the club,<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> and the transfer was completed on 3 August, when he signed a four-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He made his first appearance for Juventus in a pre-season friendly against <a href="/wiki/S.L._Benfica" title="S.L. Benfica">Benfica</a> in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a> on 1 August, coming on as a 78th-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pogba's first competitive appearance with Juventus came in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Serie_A" title="2012–13 Serie A">Serie A</a> match against <a href="/wiki/A.C._ChievoVerona" title="A.C. ChievoVerona">Chievo</a> on 22 September 2012, where he played the full 90 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> On 2 October, Pogba made his first appearance in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in a 1–1 home draw against <a href="/wiki/FC_Shakhtar_Donetsk" title="FC Shakhtar Donetsk">Shakhtar Donetsk</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> and on 20 October, Pogba scored his first goal for the club in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> On 31 October, he started against <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a> and scored the game-winning goal in a 2–1 victory. Pogba also contributed to the opening goal scored by <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Quagliarella" title="Fabio Quagliarella">Fabio Quagliarella</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> The midfielder was subsequently praised for his performance in the match by several Italian media outlets such as <i><a href="/wiki/La_Repubblica" title="La Repubblica">la Repubblica</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Il_Messaggero" title="Il Messaggero">Il Messaggero</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/La_Gazzetta_dello_Sport" title="La Gazzetta dello Sport">La Gazzetta dello Sport</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 May 2013, Pogba was sent off in Juventus' <i><a href="/wiki/List_of_Italian_football_champions" title="List of Italian football champions">Scudetto</a></i>-clinching game for spitting towards an opponent after being slapped in the face.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14_season">2013–14 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus,_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg/170px-Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="253" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg/255px-Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg/340px-Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus%2C_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1159" data-file-height="1728" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Real_Madrid_vs_Juventus,_24_October_2013_Champions_League_-_%C3%81lvaro_Arbeloa_%26_Paul_Pogba.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba (right) playing for <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>On 18 August 2013, Pogba was a key protagonist of Juventus' 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>, the match that won Juventus the <a href="/wiki/2013_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2013 Supercoppa Italiana">2013 Italian Supercoppa</a>. During the match, Pogba replaced <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Marchisio" title="Claudio Marchisio">Claudio Marchisio</a> and scored the first goal of the game; he was elected Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> In December, Pogba was named 2013's <a href="/wiki/Golden_Boy_(award)" title="Golden Boy (award)">Golden Boy</a> for the best young player in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2014, Pogba was named by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> as one of the ten most promising young players in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Guardian_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Guardian-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 20 February, Pogba scored his first goal in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_club_competitions" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA club competitions">UEFA club competitions</a> as Juventus defeated <a href="/wiki/Trabzonspor" title="Trabzonspor">Trabzonspor</a> 2–0 at home in the first leg of the round of 32 of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Europa League">2013–14 UEFA Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 14 April, Pogba produced an assist in Juventus's 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a>, the same team that Pogba scored two magnificent goals against in the previous season. Later that week, Pogba scored the only goal in Juventus's 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a>. Pogba was also named the man of the match for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-whoscored.com_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-whoscored.com-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Pogba would prove to be a key player for the club that season, breaking into the starting line-up,<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> and making more appearances (51) for the club than any other player across all competitions that season, also scoring 9 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He finished the season with his second consecutive <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Serie_A" title="2013–14 Serie A">Serie A title</a> under manager <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Conte" title="Antonio Conte">Antonio Conte</a>, also reaching the semi-finals of the Europa League.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15_season">2014–15 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus,_2014,_Paul_Pogba.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg/170px-Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="290" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg/255px-Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg/340px-Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus%2C_2014%2C_Paul_Pogba.jpg 2x" data-file-width="978" data-file-height="1668" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Singapore_Selection_vs_Juventus,_2014,_Paul_Pogba.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba playing for <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 20 September 2014, under new Juventus manager <a href="/wiki/Massimiliano_Allegri" title="Massimiliano Allegri">Massimiliano Allegri</a>, Pogba contributed to Juventus's away win against Milan by providing the assist for the only goal of the game, scored by <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Tevez" title="Carlos Tevez">Carlos Tevez</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, on 18 October, Pogba saved Juventus from a defeat against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Sassuolo_Calcio" title="U.S. Sassuolo Calcio">Sassuolo</a> by scoring a decisive equaliser; he was later named Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> On 24 October, Pogba renewed his contract with Juventus, tying him to the club until 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 4 November, on his 100th appearance with the club, Pogba scored Juventus's third goal against <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, helping them to win the match; this was his first ever Champions League goal.<sup id="cite_ref-whoscored.com_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-whoscored.com-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> On 22 November, he scored his first brace of the season in a 3–0 win against Lazio at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a> in Rome.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 28 October, Pogba was named as one of the 23 shortlisted candidates for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2014 FIFA Ballon d&#39;Or">2014 Ballon d'Or</a>; at 21, he was the youngest on the list.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, Pogba was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Bravo_Award" title="Bravo Award">Bravo Award</a>, by the Italian sports magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Guerin_Sportivo" title="Guerin Sportivo">Il Guerin Sportivo</a></i>, which is awarded to the best under-23 player who has participated in European competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-canalejuve.it_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-canalejuve.it-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 January 2015, Pogba helped Juventus secure their first win against Napoli at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_San_Paolo" title="Stadio San Paolo">Stadio San Paolo</a> in 14 years as he scored a volley that helped Juventus beat Napoli 1–3.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> On 15 January, he scored his first goal in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Coppa_Italia" title="2014–15 Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> as Juventus defeated Verona 6–1 in the round of 16 of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 9 March, Pogba scored the only goal in a 1–0 victory against Sassuolo to put Juventus 11 points clear of <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> at the top of the league table.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg of Juventus's round of 16 tie against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>, Pogba was taken off during the first half after injuring his hamstring and was later ruled out for two months.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He returned to the starting line-up on 9 May, scoring in a 1–1 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Cagliari_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Cagliari F.C.">Cagliari</a>, as Juventus celebrated winning their fourth consecutive <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Serie_A" title="2014–15 Serie A">Serie A title</a> since 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> On 13 May, Pogba set up <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Morata" title="Álvaro Morata">Álvaro Morata</a>'s equaliser against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> in the second leg of the Champions League semi-final; the goal allowed Juventus win the tie 3–2 on aggregate to advance to the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League Final</a> for the first time in 12 years.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> On 20 May, Pogba set up Juventus's first goal as they defeated Lazio 2–1 at the Stadio Olimpico in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2015 Coppa Italia Final">2015 Coppa Italia Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 6 June 2015, Pogba started for Juventus in the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">2015 UEFA Champions League Final</a> as the club were defeated 3–1 by <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> at <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_Berlin" class="mw-redirect" title="Olympiastadion Berlin">Olympiastadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span></h4>
<p>On 15 July 2015, Pogba was named to the ten-man shortlist for the 2015 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Best_Player_in_Europe_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Best Player in Europe Award">UEFA Best Player in Europe Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> For the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Juventus_F.C._season" title="2015–16 Juventus F.C. season">2015–16 season</a>, he was awarded the prestigious <a href="/wiki/Squad_number_(association_football)" title="Squad number (association football)">number-10 shirt</a>, following Carlos Tevez's departure, which had previously been worn by <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Del_Piero" title="Alessandro Del Piero">Alessandro Del Piero</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Baggio" title="Roberto Baggio">Roberto Baggio</a> and <a href="/wiki/Michel_Platini" title="Michel Platini">Michel Platini</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> On 8 August, he assisted a goal in Juventus's 2–0 win over Lazio in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2015 Supercoppa Italiana">2015 Supercoppa Italiana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> On 12 August, it was announced that he placed tenth in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Best_Player_in_Europe_Award#2014.E2.80.9315" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Best Player in Europe Award">2015 UEFA Best Player in Europe Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-UEFA_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFA-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> On 31 October, Pogba made his 100th Serie A appearance in a 2–1 home win over <a href="/wiki/Torino_F.C." title="Torino F.C.">Torino</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Turin_Derby" class="mw-redirect" title="Turin Derby">Turin Derby</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> also scoring Juventus's opening goal from a half-volley from outside the area.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> On 24 November, Pogba was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year#Team_of_the_Year_2015" title="UEFA Team of the Year">2015 UEFA Team of the Year</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> later being named to the team on 8 January 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-UEFAteam2015_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFAteam2015-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Three days later he was named to the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_World_XI" title="FIFPro">2015 FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFProteam2015_91-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFProteam2015-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Pogba excelled in his team's new creative position, which saw him gain more time on the ball, and played a key role in helping Juventus to the league title,<sup id="cite_ref-Juventus_crowned_Serie_A_champions_after_Roma_score_late_against_Napoli_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Juventus_crowned_Serie_A_champions_after_Roma_score_late_against_Napoli-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> scoring a joint personal best of 8 goals in Serie A, while also finishing the league season as the top assist provider in Serie A, with a personal record of 12 assists, alongside <a href="/wiki/Miralem_Pjani%C4%87" title="Miralem Pjani">Miralem Pjani</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-assists_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-assists-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Manchester_United">Return to Manchester United</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk,_September_2016_(07)_-_Paul_Pogba_(edited).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg/170px-Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="209" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg/255px-Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg/340px-Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk%2C_September_2016_%2807%29_-_Paul_Pogba_%28edited%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2715" data-file-height="3345" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Manchester_United_v_Zorya_Luhansk,_September_2016_(07)_-_Paul_Pogba_(edited).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba playing for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in 2016</div></div></div>
<p>On 8 August 2016, Pogba returned to former club, Manchester United, on a five-year contract for a <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">then-record for highest football transfer fee</a> at €105&#160;million (£89.3&#160;million) plus bonuses of €5&#160;million, surpassing the former record holder <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Paul Pogba's agent, <a href="/wiki/Mino_Raiola" title="Mino Raiola">Mino Raiola</a>, received a reported €27&#160;million from Juventus when he re-joined Manchester United;<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Juventus disclosed the fee as an auxiliary expense, for €26.154&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Football_Association" title="The Football Association">The Football Association</a> announced that Pogba would be suspended for Manchester United's opening Premier League fixture of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Premier_League" title="2016–17 Premier League">2016–17 season</a> against <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>, due to two yellow cards he had accumulated in the previous season's edition of the Coppa Italia with Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> On 19 August, he made his first appearance since returning to the club in a 2–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the 2–1 defeat at home in the first <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a> of the season on 10 September, Pogba was criticised for his lack of discipline in positioning by pundit <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Carragher" title="Jamie Carragher">Jamie Carragher</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> Pogba, however, soon recovered to form and scored his first <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> goal for United with a header against defending champions <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Leicester City">Leicester City</a> in a 4–1 home win on 24 September.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> He then scored twice, once from the penalty spot and then with a strike from distance, in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> tie against <a href="/wiki/Fenerbah%C3%A7e_S.K." title="Fenerbahçe S.K.">Fenerbahçe</a> on 20 October.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> Manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> defended Pogba after the game, criticising football's "<a href="/wiki/Albert_Einstein" title="Albert Einstein">Einsteins</a>" for being too quick to judge the player.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2017, Pogba scored in a 2–1 away defeat to <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a> in the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_EFL_Cup" title="2016–17 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> semi-final, which allowed Manchester United to advance to the final 3–2 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> On 24 May 2017, Pogba scored in the 18th minute of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Europa League Final">final</a> against Dutch club <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">AFC Ajax</a>, which proved to be the game-winning goal as Manchester United defeated Ajax 2–0 to win United's first continental trophy in nine years.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> Manchester United finished the 2016–17 Premier League season in sixth place, with Pogba being involved in 30 games, scoring five goals and providing four assists.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span></h4>
<p>Pogba scored the fourth goal in a 4–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a> on the opening weekend of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Premier_League" title="2017–18 Premier League">2017–18 Premier League</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> During a 3–0 defeat of <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League group stage">2017–18 UEFA Champions League group stage</a>, Pogba tore his left hamstring and was expected to miss eight matches.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> He returned to action on 18 November in a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a>, assisting <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Martial" title="Anthony Martial">Anthony Martial</a> with a cross from the flank and scored United's third goal.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> In his first game of 2018, on 1 January, Pogba provided assists for both goals as Manchester United defeated <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Throughout the next few months, Pogba was again the subject of criticism regarding a lack of discipline and for not fulfilling his defensive duties.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> He was absent from several pivotal games in favour of <a href="/wiki/Scott_McTominay" title="Scott McTominay">Scott McTominay</a>, including Manchester United's 2–1 victory over rivals <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> and was only used as a late substitution as his side were eliminated from the Champions League in the round of 16 by <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in March.<sup id="cite_ref-Dobson_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dobson-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The day before the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> manager <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> claimed that Pogba's agent, <a href="/wiki/Mino_Raiola" title="Mino Raiola">Mino Raiola</a>, had offered Pogba to play for his side, which Raiola denied.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> In the derby at <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">Etihad Stadium</a> on 7 April, Pogba scored two goals in quick succession as Manchester United came back to defeat their rivals 3–2 after conceding two goals in the first half. The victory also prevented Manchester City from securing the Premier League title against them, which they later did as Manchester United finished the season as runners-up.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FA_Cup_Final" title="2018 FA Cup Final">2018 FA Cup Final</a> against Chelsea, his side were defeated 1–0, with Pogba squandering a chance to equalise with a header in the penalty box.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span></h4>
<p>Due to the absence of team captain <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Valencia" title="Antonio Valencia">Antonio Valencia</a>, Pogba took over temporary captaincy of the club in the opening games of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Manchester_United_F.C._season" title="2018–19 Manchester United F.C. season">2018–19</a> season. Pogba began the season well in the first few weeks, scoring four goals as the new designated penalty taker. However following a series of disappointing results, Mourinho announced that Pogba would not captain the team again.<sup id="cite_ref-Stone1_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stone1-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> In late September, Pogba and Mourinho were filmed having a confrontation during a training session, despite Mourinho's assertion that there was "no problem" between the two.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Pogba continued to play in the starting eleven and scored in United's 2–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> However, following a spell of poor form and strained relationship with Mourinho, Pogba found himself benched and linked with an exit from Manchester United during the January transfer season.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> Continuing tentions between Pogba and Mourinho saw him branded a "virus" who influenced United's bad form by the manager.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> Pogba continued to be benched throughout the next few games up until and including United's match against Liverpool where Manchester United lost 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Shortly after this match however Mourinho was sacked as Manchester United manager,<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a> was appointed as the caretaker manager one day later.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Under new manager, Ole Gunnar Solskjær, Pogba saw a revival in his form as he scored twice consecutively against <a href="/wiki/Huddersfield_Town_A.F.C." title="Huddersfield Town A.F.C.">Huddersfield Town</a><sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> In January 2019, Pogba assisted <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Rashford" title="Marcus Rashford">Marcus Rashford</a>'s game-winning goal against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> with consecutive goals in the following matches against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> Pogba then scored a brace in a 3–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a> and was named man of the match;<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> his two goals brought his seasonal tally to a personal best of 11 league goals and 13 in all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> Pogba continued this trend by scoring again in United's <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> fifth round tie against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> where United won 2–0<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> and got an assist in a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Pogba's form dipped towards the end of the season as Manchester United only won 2 of their last 12 games of the season as they were knocked out of the FA cup by <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Pogba was also criticised for his performance in the Champions League quarter final as Manchester United lost to <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> 4–0 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> In that poor run of games, Pogba did manage to score a brace in a 2–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham</a>. On the final day of the Premier League season, Pogba started for Manchester United as they lost to <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City_F.C." title="Cardiff City F.C.">Cardiff City</a> 2–0 at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> and after the game, Pogba was seen talking to some fans who were throwing him abuse.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> Despite the poor end to the season, Pogba had the most productive season of his career as he scored 16 goals and got 11 assists in all competition and was named in the PFA team of the year, despite his inconsistent form.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span></h4>
<p>During the summer of 2019, Pogba hinted that his time at the club was coming to an end as he said "it could be a good time to have a new challenge somewhere else" with <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> being linked to the player.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Despite the speculation of Pogba leaving, he participated in United's preseason.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> Towards the end of July, Manchester United rejected a £27.6 million plus <a href="/wiki/James_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="James Rodríguez">James Rodríguez</a> offer from Real Madrid for Paul Pogba as they felt the offer fell way below their evaluation of the player.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pogba started for Manchester United in their opening game in the Premier League on 11 August 2019, providing two assists in the club's 4–0 home win over Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> In a post-game interview, Pogba said even though he was a Manchester United player, a "question mark" remained over his future.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> Pogba suffered <a href="/wiki/Racism_in_association_football" title="Racism in association football">racist abuse</a> on social media after missing a penalty during a 1–1 away draw against <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a> the following game.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 August, Pogba suffered an ankle injury in a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>, putting him out of action for one month. His return to the squad was in a <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_EFL_Cup" title="2019–20 EFL Cup">League Cup</a> penalty shootout win over <a href="/wiki/Rochdale_A.F.C." title="Rochdale A.F.C.">Rochdale</a>. Pogba then featured in the following game, a 1–1 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, where he suffered a recurrence of his injury but also made his 100th appearance for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> In late October it was announced that due to his injury, he would be out until December 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> In December 2019 his return was delayed by illness.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> Pogba made two appearances from the bench in late December against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a> and <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> before suffering a second recurrence of his August injury. In January 2020, Pogba underwent surgery on his ankle putting him out of action for a further four to eight weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2020, manager <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskjær">Ole Gunnar Solskjær</a> announced that Pogba would be fit to play following the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League#Effects_of_the_COVID-19_pandemic" title="2019–20 Premier League">return to football during project restart</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> In United's first game of the restart, Pogba came on as a substitute and won a penalty which <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Fernandes_(footballer,_born_1994)" class="mw-redirect" title="Bruno Fernandes (footballer, born 1994)">Bruno Fernandes</a> converted, resulting in a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> On 24 June, Pogba made his first start since September in a 3–0 crushing of <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_United_F.C." title="Sheffield United F.C.">Sheffield United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 July, Pogba scored his first goal of the season as United won 3–0 at <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span></h4>
<p>Pogba scored his first goal of the 2020–21 season against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a> in the fourth round of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_EFL_Cup" title="2020–21 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> on 30 September 2020, scoring from a deflected free kick to give United a 3–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pogba_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="274" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Pogba_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1009" data-file-height="1628" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pogba_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba with the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-19_football_team" title="France national under-19 football team">France national under-19 team</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2012_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a></div></div></div>
<p>Pogba began his international career for France with the <a href="/wiki/France_national_youth_football_team" title="France national youth football team">national youth football team</a> and earned caps at all levels for which he was eligible. Prior to his international debut, Pogba was named <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> of the under-16 team by coach Guy Ferrier. He made his youth international debut on 23 September 2008 in the team's opening match of the campaign against <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_football_team" title="Wales national football team">Wales</a> in <a href="/wiki/Llanelli" title="Llanelli">Llanelli</a>. France won the match 4–2.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> Under Pogba's leadership, the team recorded impressive victories over <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> and <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a> in the Tournoi du <a href="/wiki/Val-de-Marne" title="Val-de-Marne">Val-de-Marne</a> and defeated the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a> by an aggregate score of 8–2 over the course of two matches.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> On 31 January 2009, he scored his first youth international goal in the 2009 Aegean Cup Final against <a href="/wiki/Norway_national_football_team" title="Norway national football team">Norway</a>. The goal gave France a 1–0 lead and the team won the match 2–1 to win the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was a part of the team that played at the <a href="/wiki/2010_UEFA_European_Under-17_Championship" title="2010 UEFA European Under-17 Championship">2010 UEFA European Under-17 Championship</a> scoring both of his goals with the team at the tournament. He scored the only goal in the team's 1–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_under-17_football_team" title="Portugal national under-17 football team">Portugal</a> in the group stage and netted his second in the team's 2–1 loss to England in the semi-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> Following the departure of Ferrier as the team's youth international coach, Pogba was re-instated as captain at his age level by new coach <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Mankowski" title="Pierre Mankowski">Pierre Mankowski</a>. Mankowski had previously been the assistant manager of the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">senior national team</a> under the reign of <a href="/wiki/Raymond_Domenech" title="Raymond Domenech">Raymond Domenech</a>. Pogba made his under-18 debut on 27 October 2010 at the Tournio de Limoges against <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a> in a 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> On 24 March 2011, Pogba scored his first goal with the team netting the game-winning goal in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-18_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Germany national under-18 football team">Germany</a>. The goal was scored from over 30 metres (33&#160;yd) out.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pogba made his debut with the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-19_football_team" title="France national under-19 football team">under-19 team</a> in its first match of the season against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_under-19_football_team" title="Italy national under-19 football team">Italy</a> on 6 September 2011. In the match, he assisted on two goals, scored by <a href="/wiki/Jean-Christophe_Bahebeck" title="Jean-Christophe Bahebeck">Jean-Christophe Bahebeck</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Koura" title="Anthony Koura">Anthony Koura</a>, in a 3–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> On 29 February 2012, he scored his first goal for the team in a 2–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-19_football_team" title="Spain national under-19 football team">Spain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/2012_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship_elite_qualification" title="2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship elite qualification">Elite Round qualification</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2012_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>, Pogba scored the fifth goal in the team's 6–0 rout of the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_under-19_football_team" title="Netherlands national under-19 football team">Netherlands</a>. The victory qualified France for the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> On 11 June 2012, Pogba was named to the squad to participate in the tournament. In the team's opening group stage match against <a href="/wiki/Serbia_national_under-19_football_team" title="Serbia national under-19 football team">Serbia</a>, he converted a penalty in a 3–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> France reached the semi-finals where the team faced Spain. In the match, with France trailing 3–2 in <a href="/wiki/Extra_time" class="mw-redirect" title="Extra time">extra time</a>, Pogba scored the equalising goal three minutes prior to the match's completion to send it to <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout" title="Penalty shootout">penalties</a>. However, despite Pogba converting the opening penalty for France, <i>Les Bleuets</i> were defeated 4–2.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to the under-19 team's semi-final appearance in the 2012 UEFA European Under-19 Championship, the nation qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>, which merited <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-20_football_team" title="France national under-20 football team">under-20 team</a> appearances for Pogba. Similar to the previous two seasons, Pogba was installed as captain by Mankowski and made his under-20 debut in a 0–0 draw against <a href="/wiki/China_national_under-20_football_team" title="China national under-20 football team">China</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> In the team's next match against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_national_under-20_football_team" title="North Korea national under-20 football team">North Korea</a>, Pogba scored the team's second goal in a 3–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> Pogba was the captain of the team that won France's first ever <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2013 FIFA U-20 World Cup">FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>. In that tournament held in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, he played every minute of all of France's matches except for the final group match against Spain, in which he was an unused substitute. He was named the best player of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-Pogba_meilleur_joueur_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pogba_meilleur_joueur-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career_and_2014_World_Cup">Early career and 2014 World Cup</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg/170px-Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="184" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg/255px-Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg/340px-Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg 2x" data-file-width="735" data-file-height="796" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_-_2013_-_France.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba making his debut for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 March 2013, Pogba made his debut for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">French senior team</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualifying" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualifying">2014 World Cup qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/Georgia_national_football_team" title="Georgia national football team">Georgia</a>. He played the full 90 minutes in a 3–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first international goal against <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_football_team" title="Belarus national football team">Belarus</a> on 10 September 2013 in a 4–2 victory, once again during a 2014 World Cup qualifier.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 June 2014, Pogba was named in France's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> On 15 June, he started in central midfield in the team's first World Cup fixture – a 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_football_team" title="Honduras national football team">Honduras</a> – suffering a foul from <a href="/wiki/Wilson_Palacios" title="Wilson Palacios">Wilson Palacios</a> which led to a red card for the Honduran and a penalty kick, which was converted by <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a> to give France the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> He appeared as a substitute in the team's second match, assisting a goal for Benzema in a 5–2 victory of <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Round_of_16" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">round of 16</a>, Pogba scored a 79th minute opening goal and was named man of the match by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a><sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> as <i>Les Bleus</i> defeated <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a> 2–0 in <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">Brasília</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> France were eliminated in the quarter-finals of the competition following a 1–0 defeat to eventual champions Germany on 4 July with Pogba giving away the free kick from which the Germans eventually scored.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> On 13 July 2014, Pogba was named the tournament's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Awards" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">Best Young Player</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-hyundaiyoungplayer_182-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hyundaiyoungplayer-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2016">Euro 2016</span></h4>
<p>In May 2016, Pogba was named by national side manager <a href="/wiki/Didier_Deschamps" title="Didier Deschamps">Didier Deschamps</a> to France's 23-man squad for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>, to be played on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> Although much was expected of Pogba at the upcoming European Championships, in France's opening match of the tournament, a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a> on 10 June, he endured criticism for his perceived negative performance after being played out of position and was subsequently left on the bench by Deschamps for his nation's second group match, later coming on as a second-half substitute in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Albania_national_football_team" title="Albania national football team">Albania</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form_184-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> In the round of the 16, he was once again the target of media scrutiny for conceding an early penalty against <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Ireland</a>, prompting former England international <a href="/wiki/Gary_Lineker" title="Gary Lineker">Gary Lineker</a> to tweet: “Is Pogba the world’s most overrated player?”; France eventually came from behind to win the match 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form_184-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup>
