</p><p>In the quarter-final match against <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a> on 3 July, at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>, Pogba was able to recapture his form, putting on a dominant performance in his new midfield role, as he scored his nation's second goal of the night from a header following <a href="/wiki/Antoine_Griezmann" title="Antoine Griezmann">Antoine Griezmann</a>'s corner, which he had previously helped to obtain;<sup id="cite_ref-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form_184-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pogba_propels_five-star_France_back_into_form-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> he later started the play which led to Griezmann's goal, as the host nation advanced to the semi-finals of the competition following a 5–2 win.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-final match against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> four days later, Pogba was once again started in a deep-lying midfield role alongside <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Matuidi" title="Blaise Matuidi">Blaise Matuidi</a> in a 4–2–3–1 formation; following <a href="/wiki/N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9" title="N&#39;Golo Kanté">N'Golo Kanté</a>'s introduction in the second half, he was shifted to a more advanced role, which gave him more tactical freedom, and he subsequently helped to create Griezmann's second goal of the match, as the hosts defeated the reigning World Cup Champions 2–0 to advance to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2016 Final">final</a> of the tournament,<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> where they suffered a 1–0 extra-time defeat to Portugal.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup_victory">2018 World Cup victory</span></h4>
<p>On 17 May 2018, Pogba was named in the France squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> On 16 June 2018, he took the shot that deflected off <a href="/wiki/Aziz_Behich" title="Aziz Behich">Aziz Behich</a> and resulted in the winning goal in France's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_soccer_team" title="Australia national soccer team">Australia</a> in their opening match at the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> The goal was initially awarded to Pogba, but the following day FIFA re-awarded it as an own goal to Behich.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the 59th minute of the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">2018 FIFA World Cup Final</a>, Pogba extended France's lead over <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a> to 3–1 with a strike from the edge of the penalty area after his initial shot had been blocked.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> France eventually won the World Cup by a score of 4–2.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg/170px-Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="222" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg/255px-Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f0/Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg/340px-Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1127" data-file-height="1469" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_Pogba_2017-03-09.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pogba playing for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Primarily a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, although he is also capable of playing on the <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">left</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Holding_midfielder" title="Midfielder">holding</a> role, as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deep-lying playmaker</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Box-to-box_midfielder" title="Midfielder">box-to-box role</a>, or even as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Paul_Pogba_(Manchester_United_FC)_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Paul_Pogba_(Manchester_United_FC)-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around_194-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> Pogba has been described by his club Manchester United as a "powerful, skilful, and creative" player who has "an eye for goal and a penchant for the spectacular."<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> He is also capable of playing as an offensive–minded central midfielder, who will often drift out wide, known as the "<a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Mezzala" title="Midfielder">mezzala</a>" role in Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> During his time in Italy, he gained the nicknames <i>Il Polpo Paul</i> ("<a href="/wiki/Paul_the_Octopus" title="Paul the Octopus">Paul the Octopus</a>") for his long legs that look like tentacles during tackling or running<sup id="cite_ref-festa_199-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-festa-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> and "Pogboom" for his explosive playing style and energy on the pitch.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> A large, quick, hard-working and physically strong player, he excels in the air and is also known for his stamina, as well as his powerful and accurate striking ability from distance; he has also drawn praise for his finesse, technique, flair and <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills,<sup id="cite_ref-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around_194-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Five_ways_Paul_Pogba_has_improved_since_his_first_stint_with_Man_United_201-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Five_ways_Paul_Pogba_has_improved_since_his_first_stint_with_Man_United-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Is_he_worth_the_hype?_The_best_Pogba_stats_ahead_of_Man_United_return_202-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Is_he_worth_the_hype?_The_best_Pogba_stats_ahead_of_Man_United_return-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> as well as his ability to hold up the ball.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> His characteristics and playing role in <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfield</a> initially led him to be compared with former France international <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Vieira" title="Patrick Vieira">Patrick Vieira</a> in his youth.<sup id="cite_ref-festa_199-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-festa-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During his final season with Juventus, Pogba was deployed in a more advanced and creative midfield role rather than in his usual box-to-box role,<sup id="cite_ref-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around_194-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Juve&#39;s_Paul_Pogba_pressing_his_claim_as_the_best_box-to-box_midfielder_around-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> which saw him gain more time on the ball, and he excelled as the team's main <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a>, due to his vision and passing range;<sup id="cite_ref-Juventus_crowned_Serie_A_champions_after_Roma_score_late_against_Napoli_92-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Juventus_crowned_Serie_A_champions_after_Roma_score_late_against_Napoli-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Five_ways_Paul_Pogba_has_improved_since_his_first_stint_with_Man_United_201-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Five_ways_Paul_Pogba_has_improved_since_his_first_stint_with_Man_United-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Is_he_worth_the_hype?_The_best_Pogba_stats_ahead_of_Man_United_return_202-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Is_he_worth_the_hype?_The_best_Pogba_stats_ahead_of_Man_United_return-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> his performances in this role saw him develop from a promising youngster into one of the best and most complete midfielders in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> Upon Pogba's departure from Juventus in 2016, his former teammate <a href="/wiki/Gianluigi_Buffon" title="Gianluigi Buffon">Gianluigi Buffon</a> compared him to French former playmakers <a href="/wiki/Michel_Platini" title="Michel Platini">Michel Platini</a> and <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, and also praised his ability, leadership, work-rate and attitude, both on the pitch and in training, stating that he "...is a tremendous warrior on the pitch but also has so much talent. His control of the ball and the way he can swiftly change the play from defence to attack is special."<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> Pogba is also an effective <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty taker</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media_and_sponsorships">Media and sponsorships</span></h2>
<p>Pogba has a sponsorship deal with sportswear and equipment supplier <a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a>. He wears <a href="/wiki/Adidas_Predator" title="Adidas Predator">Adidas Predator</a> football boots which he has promoted in commercials.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> He appeared in an Adidas 2018 World Cup commercial along with other players in the Adidas stable, including <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David Beckham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mohamed_Salah" title="Mohamed Salah">Mohamed Salah</a>, as well as American singer <a href="/wiki/Pharrell_Williams" title="Pharrell Williams">Pharrell Williams</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Appearing in <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>, Pogba's <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a>, '<a href="/wiki/Dab_(dance)" title="Dab (dance)">the Dab</a>', was first featured in <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_17" title="FIFA 17">FIFA 17</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> Pogba, with his brothers <a href="/wiki/Florentin_Pogba" title="Florentin Pogba">Florentin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mathias_Pogba" title="Mathias Pogba">Mathias</a>, attended the <a href="/wiki/2017_MTV_Europe_Music_Awards" title="2017 MTV Europe Music Awards">2017 MTV Europe Music Awards</a> in London, where Paul and English actress <a href="/wiki/Natalie_Dormer" title="Natalie Dormer">Natalie Dormer</a> presented the "Best Song" award to Canadian singer <a href="/wiki/Shawn_Mendes" title="Shawn Mendes">Shawn Mendes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

	<h3 id="p-personal-label" class="vector-menu-heading">
